--
-- Name: addbargraphtonote(boolean, text, text, spoff_value_type); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION addbargraphtonote(cond boolean, doc text, valname text, value spoff_value_type) RETURNS boolean
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
if cond==False:
        if "barGraphList" not in GD[doc].keys():
                #first textunder
                GD[doc]["barGraphList"] = {}
if value['part_id'] not in GD[doc]["barGraphList"]:
        GD[doc]["barGraphList"][value['part_id']] = {}
if value['voice'] not in GD[doc]["barGraphList"][value['part_id']]:
        GD[doc]["barGraphList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']] = []
if valname not in GD[doc]["barGraphList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']]:
        GD[doc]["barGraphList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']].append(valname)
GD[doc]["noteData"][value["work_id"]][value["note_id"]][valname] = value['value']
return True
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.addbargraphtonote(cond boolean, doc text, valname text, value spoff_value_type) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: addlinegraphtonote(boolean, text, text, spoff_value_type); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION addlinegraphtonote(cond boolean, doc text, valname text, value spoff_value_type) RETURNS boolean
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
if cond==False:
        if "lineGraphList" not in GD[doc].keys():
                #first textunder
                GD[doc]["lineGraphList"] = {}
        GD[doc]["lineGraphList"][value['part_id']] = {}
        GD[doc]["lineGraphList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']] = []
        GD[doc]["lineGraphList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']].append(valname)
if value['part_id'] not in GD[doc]["lineGraphList"]:
        GD[doc]["lineGraphList"][value['part_id']] = {}
if value['voice'] not in GD[doc]["lineGraphList"][value['part_id']]:
        GD[doc]["lineGraphList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']] = [valname]
if valname in GD[doc]["noteData"][value["work_id"]][value["note_id"]]:
        GD[doc]["noteData"][value["work_id"]][value["note_id"]][valname].append(value['value'])
else:
        GD[doc]["noteData"][value["work_id"]][value["note_id"]][valname] = list()
return True
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.addlinegraphtonote(cond boolean, doc text, valname text, value spoff_value_type) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: addscorenotetodocument(boolean, text, score_notes); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION addscorenotetodocument(cond boolean, doc text, note score_notes) RETURNS boolean
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
if cond==False:
        #we are starting a new document so we clear the global dictionary entry
        GD[doc] = {}
        GD[doc]["noteData"] = {}
if note["work_id"] not in GD[doc]["noteData"].keys():
        GD[doc]["noteData"][note["work_id"]] = {}
GD[doc]["noteData"][note.pop("work_id")][note.pop("note_id")] = note
return True
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.addscorenotetodocument(cond boolean, doc text, note score_notes) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: addtexttonote(boolean, text, text, spoff_value_type); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION addtexttonote(cond boolean, doc text, valname text, value spoff_value_type) RETURNS boolean
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
if cond==False:
        if "textUnderList" not in GD[doc].keys():
                #first textunder
                GD[doc]["textUnderList"] = {}
        GD[doc]["textUnderList"][value['part_id']] = {}
        GD[doc]["textUnderList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']] = []
        GD[doc]["textUnderList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']].append(valname)
if value['part_id'] not in GD[doc]["textUnderList"]:
        GD[doc]["textUnderList"][value['part_id']] = {}
if value['voice'] not in GD[doc]["textUnderList"][value['part_id']]:
        GD[doc]["textUnderList"][value['part_id']][value['voice']] = [valname]
if valname in GD[doc]["noteData"][value["work_id"]][value["note_id"]]:
        GD[doc]["noteData"][value["work_id"]][value["note_id"]][valname].extend(value['value'])
else:
        GD[doc]["noteData"][value["work_id"]][value["note_id"]][valname] = list(value['value'])
return True
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.addtexttonote(cond boolean, doc text, valname text, value spoff_value_type) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: addtime(spoff_score_time, spoff_score_time); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION addtime(t1 spoff_score_time, t2 spoff_score_time) RETURNS spoff_score_time
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
from fractions import Fraction
fraction1 = Fraction(t1['crotchet_numerator'], t1['crotchet_denominator'])
fraction2 = Fraction(t2['crotchet_numerator'], t2['crotchet_denominator'])
result = fraction1+fraction2
return {'crotchet_numerator': result.numerator, 'crotchet_denominator': result.denominator}
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.addtime(t1 spoff_score_time, t2 spoff_score_time) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: comparepitch(spoff_pitch, spoff_pitch); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION comparepitch(p1 spoff_pitch, p2 spoff_pitch) RETURNS integer
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    IMMUTABLE
    RETURNS NULL ON NULL INPUT
    AS $$
from spoff import greaterThanPitch, lessThanPitch, equatePitch
print
print p1
print p2
# Postgresql's autovacuum uses this function
# So it's going to get called with rests as p1 and p2.
# We aren't allowed to return None.
# So we define: two rests have the same pitch;
#               a rest is lower than a pitch.
# The test for a "rest" here is that the pitch is None

if p1['pitch'] == None or p2['pitch'] == None :
    if p1['pitch'] == None and p2['pitch'] == None :
        return 0
    elif p1['pitch'] != None :
        return 1
    else :
        return -1

if greaterThanPitch(p1,p2):
    print "greaterThanPitch returned", greaterThanPitch(p1,p2)
    return 1
elif lessThanPitch(p1,p2):
    print "lessThanPitch returned", lessThanPitch(p1,p2)
    return -1
elif equatePitch(p1,p2):
    print "equatePitch returned", equatePitch(p1,p2)
    return 0
else:
    print "comparepitch:"
    print p1
    print p2
    print "first value is neither less than, equal to or greater than the second"
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.comparepitch(p1 spoff_pitch, p2 spoff_pitch) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: comparetime(spoff_score_time, spoff_score_time); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION comparetime(t1 spoff_score_time, t2 spoff_score_time) RETURNS integer
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
from spoff import greaterThanTime, lessThanTime, equateTime
if greaterThanTime(t1, t2):
        return 1
elif lessThanTime (t1, t2):
        return -1
elif equateTime(t1, t2):
        return 0
else:
        return False
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.comparetime(t1 spoff_score_time, t2 spoff_score_time) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: spoff_interval(text, boolean); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION spoff_interval(text, boolean) RETURNS SETOF spoff_interval_type
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
tablename, ordered = args

plan = plpy.prepare("SELECT * FROM %s" % tablename)

ALTER FUNCTION public.spoff_interval(text, boolean) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: spoff_timed_interval(text, text); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION spoff_timed_interval(text, text) RETURNS SETOF spoff_timed_interval_type
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
from spoff import getSimultaneous
source_table_name, dest_table_name = args
plan = plpy.prepare("SELECT * FROM %s" % source_table_name)
source_table = plpy.execute(plan)

plan = plpy.prepare("SELECT * FROM %s" % dest_table_name)
dest_table = plpy.execute(plan)

for source_note in source_table:
	dest_notes = getSimultaneous(source_note, dest_table)

$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.spoff_timed_interval(text, text) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: subtracttime(spoff_score_time, spoff_score_time); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION subtracttime(t1 spoff_score_time, t2 spoff_score_time) RETURNS boolean
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
from fractions import Fraction
fraction1 = Fraction(t1['crotchet_numerator'], t1['crotchet_denominator'])
fraction2 = Fraction(t2['crotchet_numerator'], t2['crotchet_denominator'])
result = fraction1-fraction2
return {'crotchet_numerator': result.numerator, 'crotchet_denominator': result.denominator}
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.subtracttime(t1 spoff_score_time, t2 spoff_score_time) OWNER TO pgsuper;

-- Name: testargs(integer, integer, integer); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper

CREATE FUNCTION testargs(i1 integer, i2 integer, i3 integer) RETURNS integer
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
return i1+i2*i3
$$;

--
-- Name: testpy(integer[]); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE FUNCTION testpy(v integer[]) RETURNS integer[]
    LANGUAGE plpythonu
    AS $$
return eval(v.replace('{', '[').replace('}', ']'))
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.testpy(v integer[]) OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: spoff_pitch_ops; Type: OPERATOR CLASS; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE OPERATOR CLASS spoff_pitch_ops
    DEFAULT FOR TYPE spoff_pitch USING btree AS
    OPERATOR 1 <(spoff_pitch,spoff_pitch) ,
    OPERATOR 2 <=(spoff_pitch,spoff_pitch) ,
    OPERATOR 3 =(spoff_pitch,spoff_pitch) ,
    OPERATOR 4 >=(spoff_pitch,spoff_pitch) ,
    OPERATOR 5 >(spoff_pitch,spoff_pitch) ,
    FUNCTION 1 comparepitch(spoff_pitch,spoff_pitch);


ALTER OPERATOR CLASS public.spoff_pitch_ops USING btree OWNER TO pgsuper;

--
-- Name: spoff_score_time_ops; Type: OPERATOR CLASS; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper
--

CREATE OPERATOR CLASS spoff_score_time_ops
    DEFAULT FOR TYPE spoff_score_time USING btree AS
    OPERATOR 1 <(spoff_score_time,spoff_score_time) ,
    OPERATOR 2 <=(spoff_score_time,spoff_score_time) ,
    OPERATOR 3 =(spoff_score_time,spoff_score_time) ,
    OPERATOR 4 >=(spoff_score_time,spoff_score_time) ,
    OPERATOR 5 >(spoff_score_time,spoff_score_time) ,
    FUNCTION 1 comparetime(spoff_score_time,spoff_score_time);


ALTER OPERATOR CLASS public.spoff_score_time_ops USING btree OWNER TO pgsuper;

--

--

CREATE TABLE score (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    publisher character(10),
    version smallint,
    file bytea,
    mime_type character(10)
);


ALTER TABLE public.score OWNER TO pgsuper;

SET default_with_oids = false;

--
-- Name: segments; Type: TABLE; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper; Tablespace: 
--

CREATE TABLE segments (
    id integer NOT NULL,
    type text,
    file integer,
    start_location integer[],
    end_location integer[],
    start_time numeric,
    duration numeric,
    pitch spoff_pitch,
    freq numeric,
    midi_note smallint,
    align text,
    matched_note_id integer,
    matched_work_id integer,
    tuning tuning_type,
    perf_id integer,
    perfpart integer,
    midi_velocity smallint,
    centsdiff numeric
);


ALTER TABLE public.segments OWNER TO pgsuper;

-- Name: segments_id_seq; Type: SEQUENCE; Schema: public; Owner: pgsuper

    START WITH 1
    INCREMENT BY 1
    NO MAXVALUE
    NO MINVALUE
    CACHE 1;
